<h1 class='sr-only'>ngosang/trackerslist</h1>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Notes</h3><a id="user-content-notes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Notes" href="#notes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<li>A bot automatically checks the trackers and updates the lists.</li>

<li>Trackers with the same domain or pointing to the same IP address are removed. Check out the <a href="/ngosang/trackerslist/blob/master/blacklist.txt">blacklist</a>.</li>

<li>Trackers are sorted by popularity and latency (from best to worst).</li>

<li>WebSocket trackers (AKA WebTorrent, ws, wss) are supported by few clients. <a href="https://webtorrent.io" rel="nofollow">More info</a>.</li>

<li>Lists with IP addresses can be shorter because <a href="https://www.cloudflare.com/ips/" rel="nofollow">Cloudflare IPs</a> are removed.</li>
